### 2. Couture Cottagecore 时尚大片提示词

**Author**: [Zara](https://x.com/ZaraIrahh)  **Date**: 2026-01-21  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一张超现实、高级时装编辑照片：一位身穿“高级定制田园风”服装（青色和金色紧身胸衣，芥末色塔夫绸裙）的女性，坐在一片黄色野花田中，强调黄金时段光线和深景深虚化效果。

![Couture Cottagecore 时尚大片提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063228088_xstwuj_G_Jl8swW4AEZ3z0.jpg)

```
Using the uploaded image, Create an ultra-realistic, high-fashion editorial photograph of a stunning woman with long, flowing rich dark brown hair and striking blue or green eyes.

Model & Pose:

The model is seated gracefully amidst a dense field of small, luminous buttercup-yellow wildflowers and tall emerald-green grass. Her expression is dreamy and ethereal, looking off-camera with a gentle, soft smile. Her hands are delicately clasped in her lap. The style should be lifelike with incredible detail in the skin texture, hair strands, and fabric.

Outfit (Couture Cottagecore):

She is wearing a modern interpretation of a folkloric gown: a crisp, ivory peasant blouse layered under a structured, silk-brocade bodice in a rich deep teal and antique gold pattern. The ensemble includes a voluminous skirt blending textures of linen and a saturated mustard-yellow taffeta that harmonizes with the background flowers. Subtle, heirloom-quality gold jewelry (tiny hoops, delicate rings).

Photography & Style:

Shot on a medium-format film camera (e.g., Hasselblad or Contax 645).

Lighting: Soft, directional Golden Hour lighting, with a rich, luminous quality that makes the dark brown hair catch subtle highlights and the yellow flowers glow intensely.

Focus: Extremely sharp focus on the model's eyes and the texture of her bodice, with a deep, creamy bokeh (shallow depth of field) in the immediate foreground and background.

Aesthetic Presets & Filters:

High resolution, professional color grading, cinematic, dramatic clarity, Kodak Portra 800 film grain, saturated warm tones, Vsco C1 filter for added warmth and slight desaturation of greens. Vibrant, detailed, painterly quality.

Do not change the face
```

[[Golden Hour Photography]] [[High Fashion Editorial]]

### 9. Golden Hour 校服“摇滚”肖像

### 51. 电影之夜出租车人像，青色和橙色调色

### 66. 角色生成提示（步骤 1）

**Author**: [iX](https://x.com/iX00AI)  **Date**: 2026-02-12  **Language**: en

> 这是多步骤流程的第一步，此提示旨在生成一张高分辨率（建议 4K）的主角图像，重点是构图、高对比度照明，以及一位具有 K-pop 偶像美学的年轻日本女性的细致面部特征。

![角色生成提示（步骤 1）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770964577240_tfxnoo_HA9j2KxboAEwB_P.jpg)

```
I. Composition & Spatial Layout
1.Framing & Scale: The subject occupies approximately 60–70% of the frame height. Leave at least 30% of the frame height as empty space above the head. Both left and right sides retain clearly visible empty wall space.
2.Visual Focus: A minimal, uncluttered background designed to strongly emphasize facial structure, eye expression, and skin quality.

II. Lighting & Shadow Style
1.Key Light: Intense natural daylight, side-backlit with a slight reverse angle, cool-toned, producing extreme high-contrast separation between highlights and shadows.
2.Light Characteristics: Dense, hard-edged leaf-shadow patterns projected across the wall and the subject’s body and face. Shadow edges are razor-sharp with extremely narrow penumbra.
3.Highlight Control: Large areas of the background are deliberately overexposed while retaining faint surface texture, creating a glowing, almost blinding spatial atmosphere.

III. Subject Appearance (Face & Hair — Reference Applied)
1.Facial Structure:
A young Japanese woman in her 20s with a refined V-shaped face, sharp jawline, and high-definition facial contours. Overall facial balance is elegant yet striking, with high visual impact.
2.Skin Quality:
Porcelain-toned Japanese skin with a cool undertone. Ultra-smooth, luminous texture enhanced by strong contrast lighting while retaining realistic skin detail.
3.Eyes & Expression:
・Large, sharp fox-shaped eyes
・Confident gaze directed straight into the camera
・Expression carries a cool, playful, slightly teasing energy
・K-pop idol–inspired eyeliner with clearly emphasized aegyosal
・Overall expression is controlled, calm, and subtly provocative rather than smiling
4.Mouth:
Relaxed lips with a subtle, effortless smirk. Glossy gradient lips with a refined sheen, never exaggerated.
5.Hair Style:
Long, sleek, straight black hair reaching the waist, with perfectly straight, neatly trimmed Japanese bangs. Hair finish is glossy, clean, and fashion-forward, moving minimally in the light.
6.Makeup Style:
High-contrast K-pop idol–inspired makeup. Clean base, sculpted facial structure, cool-toned color balance, no warm or heavy blush.
7.Accessories (Minimal):
・Small gold pendant necklace
・Small gold hoop earrings
・Minimalist tattoo on the left inner forearm

IV. Clothing
・Cropped pure-white bandeau-style tube top
・Body-hugging but not tight, exposing the waist
・Fabric remains clean and structured, no wrinkles distracting from silhouette
```

[[High Contrast Lighting]] [[Character Design]] [[K-Pop Aesthetic]]

**Author**: [Meem](https://x.com/mehvishs25)  **Date**: 2026-03-13  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一个 16 格的黑白大头照网格，要求与参考图像高度相似，同时描绘 16 种不同的面部表情，重点突出模拟颗粒感、高对比度和特定的相机设置。

```
Create a black-and-white photobooth 4×4 expression grid using the reference image as the main anchor. The same woman’s identity, facial features, and hairstyle must be preserved with very high similarity across all panels.
The final image should be square (1:1), ultra-high resolution, arranged as a 16-panel grid with thin spacing. Each panel is a tight head-and-shoulders shot (50mm look) with sharp eyes. Use a plain gray background, direct front photobooth flash, soft short shadows, and subtle analog black-and-white grain with medium-high contrast.
She should wear a simple modest top (no logos) with natural makeup and consistent hairstyle.
Each panel shows a different expression: scrunched smile, intense stare with fingers framing eyes, big laugh, bored face with chin in hands, sad pout, goofy horns gesture, tongue-out grin, angry glare, flirty cheek touch, surprised wide eyes, excited shout with hands near face, mischievous claw pose, confused frown, dramatic crying with hands on head, playful eyes-closed tongue out, duck face with small devil horns gesture.
Avoid distorted anatomy, extra fingers, plastic skin, blur, text, logos, or color.
```

> 一个复杂的提示，用于生成一张超现实主义全身照片，照片中包含用户的肖像和他们自己的 Q 版动漫形象，并叠加 Apple Music 播放器 UI 界面，强调高对比度、特定服装以及图形元素的干净整合。

![超写实自画像，带 Q 版人物和 UI 叠加提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772692202777_5oqkbi_HCmrkYmawAI_23l.jpg)
![超写实自画像，带 Q 版人物和 UI 叠加提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772692202787_b8bmcr_HCmrkYQbAAAVLRE.jpg)

```
Create an Ultra-detailed, ratio 4:5, hyperrealistic full-body photograph of a stylish me posing on a modern city sidewalk under bright, direct midday sun. The composition is a vertical medium-full shot from an eye-level perspective. The me leans casually against a dark grey metal street pole that creates a strong vertical line just right of center. He wears a striking, slightly glossy crimson red faux leather jacket zipped halfway over a crisp white collared shirt. His trousers are wide-leg, cream-colored corduroy with visible texture. He wears polished black leather loafers. His pose is relaxed, with one leg crossed over the other, and his left hand is tucked into his pocket. He has curly black hair and wears modern black-framed glasses, looking off to his right with a neutral, cool expression. To his right, a cute chibi anime character version of himself, with a large head and big eyes, perfectly mirrors his pose and outfit, rendered with clean black line art and simple cell shading. On the left side of the frame, a large, semi-transparent, dark grey, rounded rectangle overlay mimicking an Apple Music player Ul is professionally superimposed, featuring album art of a red canoe on water and playback controls; this Ul has a subtle 'glassmorphism' frosted glass effect. The lighting is hard sunlight from the top-right, casting sharp, defined shadows on the light grey tiled pavement. The background consists of a modern building with large, greenish-tinted glass panels. Shot with a 35mm lens, f/5.6 aperture, creating sharp focus on the subject and graphics with a slightly soft background. The color science emphasizes high contrast between the crimson red, cream, and cool tones of the environment. Avoid any motion blur, unnatural skin textures, or distorted proportions. The integration of the graphic elements must be seamless and clean, without pixelation or rough edges.
```

      "source": "EXACTLY AS IN REFERENCE PHOTO",

  },

  },

[CLOTHING EXACT MATCH]: No changes to fit or material. Expression: serious, tense, focused, looking up and away. Background: Saturated solid orange-red, smooth intense gradients, hot atmosphere. ### 115. 超精细光剑角色扮演胶片摄影提示词

> 一个巨型、高度技术化的中文提示，用于生成一张高分辨率的电影照片，内容是一位角色扮演者扮演《Fate/stay night》中的 Saber。该提示使用了详尽的视觉效果列表、灯光技术（伦勃朗光、强侧光）、电影级品质（动态模糊、高对比度、胶片颗粒）和艺术风格（西方梦核、前卫视觉艺术），以实现一种强烈、神圣和冷峻的美学。

### 120. 多元时尚编辑网格

**Author**: [gokaygokay](https://x.com/gokayfem)  **Date**: 2025-12-18  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的提示，旨在生成一个 6x6 的网格，其中包含 36 位穿着相同参考服装的独特个体。该提示明确地在年龄、体型、种族、发型和面部特征方面最大化了人类多样性，要求采用不同的姿势和摄像机角度，以创作出具有包容性、高对比度的时尚大片。

![多元时尚编辑网格](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766237838133_1ji4ug_G8dksXyWwAE_bke.jpg)
![多元时尚编辑网格](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766237839176_yeakax_G8dkvNsWoAEMSaL.jpg)
![多元时尚编辑网格](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766237841328_p4dajj_G8dk4hFX0AEvL5f.jpg)
![多元时尚编辑网格](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766237841801_9s6ebq_G8dlFI_WwAA7CKK.jpg)

```
6x6 grid layout. Editorial fashion photography. Use the reference clothing item on all 36 models. Every single cell must feature a completely unique individual—no two people should look remotely similar.
Maximize human diversity across:
Age: Teenagers, 20s, 30s, 40s, 50s, 60s, 70s, 80s+, elderly with wrinkles and grey hair
Body types: Extremely thin, slim, athletic, muscular, stocky, chubby, fat, plus-size, obese, petite, tall, short, broad-shouldered, narrow-framed, pear-shaped, apple-shaped, hourglass, rectangular, long-limbed, short-limbed.
Ethnicity & skin tones: East Asian, Southeast Asian, South Asian, Middle Eastern, North African, Sub-Saharan African, West African, East African, Indigenous Australian, Pacific Islander, Native American, Indigenous South American, Scandinavian, Mediterranean, Eastern European, Western European, Caribbean, mixed race, albino. Full spectrum of skin tones from the palest to the deepest.
Hair: Bald, shaved, buzz cut, afro, locs, braids, straight, wavy, curly, coily, long, short, grey, white, natural colors, receding hairline, thinning hair, thick full hair, hijab, head wraps, turbans.
Features: Freckles, vitiligo, acne, scars, birthmarks, moles, gap teeth, crooked teeth, big nose, small nose, wide nose, narrow nose, round face, angular face, soft jawline, strong jawline, monolid eyes, deep-set eyes, hooded eyes, big lips, thin lips, visible disabilities, prosthetics, wheelchair users, amputees.
Each cell: different pose, different camera angle. Poses should feel editorial and unexpected—leaning, crouching, mid-stride, arched, sprawled, seated, jumping, twisting, lounging. Camera angles vary—low angle, overhead, Dutch tilt, wide shot, tight crop, ground-level, profile, three-quarter view.
Moody, high contrast, cinematic lighting. Varied environments—studio, architectural, urban, natural. Sharp detail, clothing as focal point. Final result should feel like the most inclusive, human-rich fashion editorial ever created—a true celebration of every single type of human body that exists.
```

    },

      "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
      "orientation": "portrait",

  "subject": {
    "identity": "Young woman with wavy brunette hair and fair skin",

    "attire": "Hot pink chunky cable-knit sweater with ribbed crew neck",
    "accessories": "Thin gold-rimmed round sunglasses with vibrant pink tinted lenses"
  },
  "layout": {
    "type": "2x2 photo collage",
    "total_panels": 4,
    "panels": [
      {
        "panel_id": 1,
        "expression": "Wide joyful smile, teeth showing",
        "pose": "Hands framing the face, palms facing forward"
      },
      {
        "panel_id": 2,
        "expression": "Thinking or playful pouting expression",
        "pose": "One finger resting against the lip"
      },
      {

      },
      {
        "panel_id": 4,
        "expression": "Silly, one eye winking with tongue sticking out",
        "pose": "Hand making a peace sign over one eye"
      }
    ]
  },

    "background": "Solid teal or muted turquoise studio wall",

### 171. Ultra-Photorealistic Fashion Editorial Prompt for Nano Banana Pro

**Author**: [Bananai](https://x.com/aibananai)  **Date**: 2026-01-02  **Language**: en

> This is a detailed, high-end fashion editorial prompt designed for the Nano Banana Pro model, focusing on ultra-photorealistic rendering. It specifies a complex scene featuring a slim, curvy female subject in a monochromatic brown suit, seated dynamically in a vintage black leather armchair against a sterile white cyclorama. The prompt includes extensive details on camera gear (Sony A7R V, 50mm f/1.8 GM), lighting (softbox and reflector fill), pose, expression, clothing textures (rough wool, patent leather), and mandates highly realistic skin texture with visible pores, strictly avoiding airbrushing.

![Ultra-Photorealistic Fashion Editorial Prompt for Nano Banana Pro](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508401022_0irpjg_G9ng0cVXwAAmvmX.jpg)
![Ultra-Photorealistic Fashion Editorial Prompt for Nano Banana Pro](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508400968_d91yox_G9ng0ccXcAA3gob.jpg)

```
A high-end fashion editorial photograph captured in an ultra-photorealistic style using a Sony A7R V with a 50mm f/1.8 GM lens, characterized by sharp focus and tactile textures. The scene is set in a minimalist photo studio featuring a sterile, pure white cyclorama infinity wall background with no distractions. The subject is a slim but curvy female in her mid-20s with mixed heritage and light olive skin, slouching comfortably in a vintage, oversized deep black leather armchair that features a chunky club style, worn leather creases, and a natural oily sheen. Her pose is dynamic and flexible: her torso is reclined deep into the chair and angled slightly right, her left leg is bent at the knee resting casually on the seat, while her right leg is extended vertically straight up in the air at 90 degrees with pointed toes. Her right hand rests relaxed on her stomach, while her left hand is raised to her mouth where she is provocatively biting the side of her thumb with her mouth slightly open. She displays a seductive, bored-chic expression with intense direct eye contact. She wears retro-chic square glasses with dark tortoiseshell top rims and gold wire bottoms showing slight studio light reflections. Her hair is long, sleek, straight brunette with honey balayage highlights, tucked behind her ears with realistic silky strands. Her outfit is a monochromatic textural brown suit featuring an oversized, structured chocolate brown blazer made of a rough wool weave, worn loose and unbuttoned over a crisp pale icy blue button-up shirt that is unbuttoned low revealing her décolletage with cuffs peeking out. She wears matching skin-tight chocolate brown wool tights that resemble thick textured hosiery, paired with deep burgundy patent leather stiletto pumps with a very high heel and a glossy finish. The lighting is professional studio quality with a large high front-right softbox and white reflector fill, creating diffused, flattering illumination that highlights the coarse fuzz of the wool fabric and the smooth sheen of the leather chair, casting soft natural shadows underneath. The skin texture is highly realistic with visible natural pores and a slight shine on the forehead, strictly avoiding any airbrushed or plastic appearance.
```

![时尚双重曝光反射肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767166951249_tvqhl5_G9T34BcaMAA0lNq.jpg)

```
{
  "version": "1.1",
  "description": "Create a high-fashion editorial double exposure portrait. The image should feature two distinct expressions creating a narrative contrast, bathed in a specific warm golden light flare against a cool background, with a mirrored reflection below.",
  "variables": {
    "PRIMARY_EXPRESSION": {
      "type": "string",
      "value": "Intense, direct, unyielding gaze into the camera",
      "description": "The grounded, sharp expression of the subject in the immediate foreground."
    },
    "SECONDARY_EXPRESSION": {
      "type": "string",
      "value": "A distant, melancholic look towards the left, as if lost in a fading memory or dream",
      "description": "The narrative-driven, emotive expression for the translucent, overlaid image that suggests inner thought or past versus present."
    }
  },
  "steps": [
    {
      "name": "NARRATIVE_DOUBLE_EXPOSURE",
      "goal": "Layer two images to create an emotional story, using a specific color palette for contrast.",
      "instructions": "Use the subject from the input image to create a cinematic double exposure.\n\n1.  **Primary Layer (The Present):** A sharp, high-definition portrait. The subject has the {argument name="primary expression" default="Intense, direct, unyielding gaze into the camera"}. The lighting is neutral to cool studio light, highlighting skin texture and silver accessories cleanly.\n2.  **Secondary Layer (The Inner World/Memory):** A translucent overlay, slightly offset. The subject has the {argument name="secondary expression" default="A distant, melancholic look towards the left, as if lost in a fading memory or dream"}. This layer must be heavily influenced by a **Warm Golden-Amber Editorial Light Leak** (like the golden hour filter in image_1). This warm tone should wash over the face and hair, creating a dreamlike, almost sepia-toned contrast against the cooler primary layer."
    },
    {
      "name": "MIRRORED_COMPOSITION",
      "goal": "Replicate the specific posing and reflective surface from the reference.",
      "instructions": "The subject is posed leaning forward with hands crossed over a highly polished, dark reflective surface. The primary layer (cool tones, direct gaze) must be perfectly mirrored below, adding symmetry and grounding the ethereal double exposure above."
    },
    {
      "name": "EDITORIAL_ATMOSPHERE",
      "goal": "Finalize the lighting and mood to match a high-end magazine aesthetic.",
      "instructions": "The background should be a smooth, muted cool grey/blue gradient studio wall, providing a clean backdrop that makes the warm golden flare pop. The overall feel should be moody, cinematic, and luxurious, capturing a frozen moment of introspection."
    }
  ],
  "final_goal": "Produce a single, high-fashion photographic still using double exposure. It must feature the subject with a sharp, direct gaze contrasted with a translucent, story-filled golden-amber memory overlay, all reflected in a polished surface beneath."
}
